msg:Hotel service: There is basically no service. The whole family traveled to Nanchang and checked in at the front desk. Although I redeemed my points for breakfast and confirmed with the front desk that breakfast was available when placing the order, I was still pulled by the front desk staff when I checked in. I struggled for half an hour, so it was not a good time to check in. Then I borrowed a charger and made three phone calls at different times. They all refused on the grounds that there were many guests staying and they didn't prepare so many chargers. I want to say, does such a large five-star hotel not have these? Then I ordered takeout. In fact, the child saw a robot delivering the meal to the room, and then the takeaway was unexpectedly turned away. Well, ask the service staff to help deliver it, because it was inconvenient for the child to go downstairs, so that's why. He declined due to lack of manpower and lack of time. Breakfast is a buffet. I witnessed an uncle from Northeast China who was staying with me very politely communicating with the aunt who was making rice noodles. The uncle said a few words, and the aunt replied in a bad mood. So this hotel really has no service at all.
Facilities: Apart from the large floor space, there is nothing else to say. It is far from the five-star hotel review. The door makes a rattling sound when it is opened. I think the disposable items in the room should be classified as an economical business hotel. It matches, maybe even not as good as some. The minibar was empty, nothing. The double bed room booked is actually two single beds pushed together.
To sum up, the biggest failure of this trip to Nanchang was choosing this hotel. All the service staff have negative working attitudes. In fact, the hotel has been open for a long time and the facilities are old. These are not too important. If every staff member I think you can get extra points if you face your work and your guests with a positive and enthusiastic attitude and professional professional skills. During the three days and two nights of my stay, if there was a problem that I needed help from the hotel to solve, the hotel basically couldn't solve it. It wasn't until I told the service staff that I wanted to make a complaint that the staff quickly became available, and I fell asleep after 9 p.m. , finally freed up manpower to call me and ask if there were any problems that needed to be solved. I felt speechless.
